if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '955018f40c6f022f82897dceac5879b2dee7a9fa') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '955018f40c6f022f82897dceac5879b2dee7a9fa') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2c41c06e24ceed9d9fc354d42b61b2ad5c1a7e5e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '955018f40c6f022f82897dceac5879b2dee7a9fa') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_2();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt') != '93ee8c7589bedd48b92a346c4aec2692dbfd35b5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt') !== '93ee8c7589bedd48b92a346c4aec2692dbfd35b5') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt') !== 'b178862cf8b17c8ef7789bada2c33542614a1141') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt') !== '93ee8c7589bedd48b92a346c4aec2692dbfd35b5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/02 plus color settings.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png') != 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png') !== 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png') !== '2d51ce8fd5a3002c83849db0d523a5954a628809') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png') !== 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/logo.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png') != 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png') !== 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png') !== '2d51ce8fd5a3002c83849db0d523a5954a628809') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png') !== 'd2941635a3ac1493345d4cfe9b84e751407db148') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/logo.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'd3ef226b4f73345c37fbb41520c7dbfc844705ad') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd3ef226b4f73345c37fbb41520c7dbfc844705ad') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '80632084d4e1ce931269caddf65f942ce1aa81df') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd3ef226b4f73345c37fbb41520c7dbfc844705ad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 794\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 794') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
